    <div class="image-wrapper">
        <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Gossip-Girl-Wedding-Pictures-22639197" title="See Every Gossip Girl Wedding!" class="ga-track" data-ga-category="river" data-ga-action="clickthrough">

        <div class="meta">
            <span itemprop="alternativeHeadline"><a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/TV">TV</a></span>
            <time title="Tue, 09 Apr 2013 13:48:02 -0700" datetime="2013-04-09T13:48:02-07:00" itemprop="dateCreated">
                Apr 09, 2013
            </time>
        </div>

        <div class="content">
            <h3>
                <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Gossip-Girl-Wedding-Pictures-22639197" title="See Every Gossip Girl Wedding!" class="ga-track" data-ga-category="river" data-ga-action="clickthrough">
                    <span itemprop="headline">See Every Gossip Girl Wedding!</span>
                </a>
            </h3>
            <div class="excerpt">
                Gossip Girl wrapped up just a few months ago, and despite the constant romantic drama on the show, many couples managed to make it down the aisle.
            </div>
            <div class="post-content clearfix">

                <span class="byline standard" itemprop="author">
    <span itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <span class="author-image ws-attribute" data-ws-key="author_image" data-ws-target="style" style="background-image: url(http://media2.onsugar.com/files/2013/03/11/2/3/31616/tmp_MeGUZQ.medium/i/Shannon-Vestal-avatar.jpg);" height="40" width="40"></span> <span class="ws-attribute" data-ws-key="author_byline" itemprop="name">by <a href="http://www.popsugar.com/author/Shannon%20Vestal" rel="author" itemprop="name">Shannon Vestal</a></span>
            </span>
</span>
                                    <div class="post-image">
                        <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Gossip-Girl-Wedding-Pictures-22639197" title="See Every Gossip Girl Wedding!" class="ga-track" data-ga-category="river" data-ga-action="clickthrough">
                            <img itemprop="thumbnailUrl" alt="See Every Gossip Girl Wedding!" title="See Every Gossip Girl Wedding!" src="http://media1.onsugar.com/files/2013/04/15/2/192/1922283/b6d869d30ca4cde2_Gossip-Girl-weddings-cover.xxxlarge/i/Gossip-Girl-Wedding-Pictures.jpg">
                        </a>
                    </div>
                
                <div itemprop="articleBody">
                    <p><a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/latest/gossip-girl" >Gossip Girl</a> wrapped up just a few months ago, and despite the constant romantic drama on the show, many couples managed to make it down the aisle. We were even treated to two huge nuptials in the series finale, so with <a class="sugar_inline_link" title="Latest photos and news for Wedding" href="http://www.popsugar.com/Wedding" target="_blank">wedding</a> season on the brain, we thought we'd take a stroll through <b>Gossip Girl</b>'s past and recount all the weddings on the series (whether the marriages lasted is another story). Revisit each wedding now and see what all the guests are wearing, who their dates are, and how beautiful each bride is. </p>

                </div>

                
                                                            <div class="thumbs">
                                                                                                <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Gossip-Girl-Wedding-Pictures-22639197?image_nid=22639234" class="ga-track" data-ga-category="river" data-ga-action="clickthrough">
                                        <img data-src="http://media2.onsugar.com/files/2012/04/15/4/192/1922283/0de0dfda332abf49_GO117d_0124b.smallsquare/i/Bart-Lily-Wedding.jpg" src="http://media4.onsugar.com/v2102/static/imgs/grey.gif"  alt="Bart and Lily&#039;s Wedding" class="image smallsquare  lazy" height="75" width="75" title="Bart and Lily&#039;s Wedding" /><noscript><img src="http://media2.onsugar.com/files/2012/04/15/4/192/1922283/0de0dfda332abf49_GO117d_0124b.smallsquare/i/Bart-Lily-Wedding.jpg"  alt="Bart and Lily&#039;s Wedding" class="image smallsquare " height="75" width="75" title="Bart and Lily&#039;s Wedding" /></noscript>
                                    </a>
                                                                                                                                <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Gossip-Girl-Wedding-Pictures-22639197?image_nid=22639231" class="ga-track" data-ga-category="river" data-ga-action="clickthrough">
                                        <img data-src="http://media2.onsugar.com/files/2012/04/15/4/192/1922283/7c7f478d3fc0510b_GO117d_0071b.smallsquare/i/Bart-Lily-Wedding.jpg" src="http://media4.onsugar.com/v2102/static/imgs/grey.gif"  alt="Bart and Lily&#039;s Wedding" class="image smallsquare  lazy" height="75" width="75" title="Bart and Lily&#039;s Wedding" /><noscript><img src="http://media2.onsugar.com/files/2012/04/15/4/192/1922283/7c7f478d3fc0510b_GO117d_0071b.smallsquare/i/Bart-Lily-Wedding.jpg"  alt="Bart and Lily&#039;s Wedding" class="image smallsquare " height="75" width="75" title="Bart and Lily&#039;s Wedding" /></noscript>

        <div class="content">
            <h3>
                <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Chuck-Bass-Pictures-20877799" title="He&#039;s Chuck Bass: See His Sexiest Smolders" class="ga-track" data-ga-category="river" data-ga-action="clickthrough">
                    <span itemprop="headline">He's Chuck Bass: See His Sexiest Smolders</span>
                </a>
            </h3>
            <div class="excerpt">
                One of the saddest things about Gossip Girl ending this week is that we will no longer get to see Chuck Bass try out any new smolders.
            </div>
            <div class="post-content clearfix">

                <span class="byline standard" itemprop="author">
    <span itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <span class="author-image ws-attribute" data-ws-key="author_image" data-ws-target="style" style="background-image: url(http://media2.onsugar.com/files/2013/03/11/2/3/31616/tmp_MeGUZQ.medium/i/Shannon-Vestal-avatar.jpg);" height="40" width="40"></span> <span class="ws-attribute" data-ws-key="author_byline" itemprop="name">by <a href="http://www.popsugar.com/author/Shannon%20Vestal" rel="author" itemprop="name">Shannon Vestal</a></span>

                                    <div class="post-image">
                        <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Chuck-Bass-Pictures-20877799" title="He&#039;s Chuck Bass: See His Sexiest Smolders" class="ga-track" data-ga-category="river" data-ga-action="clickthrough">
                            <img itemprop="thumbnailUrl" alt="He&#039;s Chuck Bass: See His Sexiest Smolders" title="He&#039;s Chuck Bass: See His Sexiest Smolders" src="http://media4.onsugar.com/files/2011/12/50/5/192/1922283/chuck-cover-new.xxxlarge/i/Chuck-Bass-Pictures.jpg">
                        </a>
                    </div>
                
                <div itemprop="articleBody">
                    <p>One of the saddest things about <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/latest/gossip-girl" >Gossip Girl</a> ending this week is that we will no longer get to see Chuck Bass try out any new smolders. <b>Gossip Girl</b>'s reformed bad boy has spent the last several seasons working on his expressions, whether it's a brow furrow, a scowl, or a sultry smirk. To say goodbye to the series  and the well-dressed bad boy who became a good man  here are the 50 best "I'm Chuck Bass" smolders.</p>

                <div itemprop="articleBody">
                    <p>We finally get to see the <a class="sugar_inline_link" title="Latest photos and news for Wedding" href="http://www.popsugar.com/Wedding" target="_blank">wedding</a> spread of <a class="sugar_inline_link" title="Latest photos and news for Blake Lively" href="http://www.popsugar.com/Blake-Lively" target="_blank">Blake Lively</a> and <a class="sugar_inline_link" title="Latest photos and news for Ryan Reynolds" href="http://www.popsugar.com/Ryan-Reynolds" target="_blank">Ryan Reynolds</a>'s big day in the new issue of <b><span class="nobrand">Martha Stewart</span> Weddings</b>. Blake also shared her holiday family traditions, and this time around, they include her new husband. Check it all out in this <b>PopSugar Rush</b>.</p>

                    <p>The <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Gossip-Girl-Series-Finale-Recap-26314184" >Gossip Girl series finale</a> aired this week, brimming with surprises and fun for its fans. Not least of which is the <a class="sugar_inline_link" title="Latest photos and news for Wedding" href="http://www.popsugar.com/Wedding" target="_blank">wedding</a> of the show's core couple, Chuck and Blair. It isn't Blair's first trip down the aisle (remember her big, <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Gossip-Girl-Wedding-Pictures-Blair-21259988" >fancy fairy-tale wedding</a>?), but it's far sweeter and more meaningful than her big day with the prince.             <div class="post-content clearfix">

                <span class="byline standard" itemprop="author">
    <span itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

                <div itemprop="articleBody">
                    <p><a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Gossip-Girl-Series-Finale-Recap-26314184" >Gossip Girl came to an end</a> with its final episode this week, bringing a handful of milestones with it. <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Gossip-Girl-Series-Finale-Pictures-26187387" >Blair and Chuck had a beautiful but quick wedding</a>, but the real surprise was when we jumped to the future  where Dan and Serena had some nuptials of their own!             <h3>
                <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Gossip-Girl-Series-Finale-Recap-26314184" title="Top OMG Moments From Gossip Girl Series Finale &quot;New York, I Love You XOXO&quot;" class="ga-track" data-ga-category="river" data-ga-action="clickthrough">
                    <span itemprop="headline">Top OMG Moments From Gossip Girl Series Finale "New York, I Love You XOXO"</span>
                </a>
            </h3>
            <div class="excerpt">
                Well, it's finally here.
            </div>
            <div class="post-content clearfix">

                <span class="byline standard" itemprop="author">
    <span itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <span class="author-image ws-attribute" data-ws-key="author_image" data-ws-target="style" style="background-image: url(http://media2.onsugar.com/files/2013/03/11/2/3/31616/tmp_MeGUZQ.medium/i/Shannon-Vestal-avatar.jpg);" height="40" width="40"></span> <span class="ws-attribute" data-ws-key="author_byline" itemprop="name">by <a href="http://www.popsugar.com/author/Shannon%20Vestal" rel="author" itemprop="name">Shannon Vestal</a></span>
            </span>

                        <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Gossip-Girl-Series-Finale-Recap-26314184" title="Top OMG Moments From Gossip Girl Series Finale &quot;New York, I Love You XOXO&quot;" class="ga-track" data-ga-category="river" data-ga-action="clickthrough">

                        </a>
                    </div>
                
                <div itemprop="articleBody">
                    <p>Well, it's finally here. We've reached the end of <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/latest/gossip-girl" >Gossip Girl</a>, and after this week's series finale, Gossip Girl can never say that her identity is the one secret she'll never tell. We find out exactly who's been giving us all the dirty details on the scandalous lives of Manhattan's elite, and speaking of those scandalous lives, Chuck and Blair finally tie the knot amid suspicions he murdered his own father. But I can't wait to get to all the OMG moments of the finale, including the ultimate one, so let's do this! </p>

                </div>

                    <span itemprop="headline">See the Pictures From the Gossip Girl Series Finale!</span>
                </a>
            </h3>
            <div class="excerpt">
                Gossip Girl will say goodbye to the Upper East Side and the small screen tonight, and we have all the pictures from the upcoming finale here.
            </div>
            <div class="post-content clearfix">

                <span class="byline standard" itemprop="author">
    <span itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <span class="author-image ws-attribute" data-ws-key="author_image" data-ws-target="style" style="background-image: url(http://media2.onsugar.com/files/2013/03/11/2/3/31616/tmp_MeGUZQ.medium/i/Shannon-Vestal-avatar.jpg);" height="40" width="40"></span> <span class="ws-attribute" data-ws-key="author_byline" itemprop="name">by <a href="http://www.popsugar.com/author/Shannon%20Vestal" rel="author" itemprop="name">Shannon Vestal</a></span>

</span>
                                    <div class="post-image">
                        <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Gossip-Girl-Series-Finale-Pictures-26187387" title="See the Pictures From the Gossip Girl Series Finale!" class="ga-track" data-ga-category="river" data-ga-action="clickthrough">

                        </a>
                    </div>
                
                <div itemprop="articleBody">
                    <p><a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/latest/gossip-girl" >Gossip Girl</a> will say goodbye to the Upper East Side and the small screen tonight, and we have all the pictures from the upcoming finale here. We already had a peek at the <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Gossip-Girl-Blair-Chuck-Wedding-Pictures-25471530" >wedding-filled event</a>, and now you can see even more, like Chuck and Blair's road to the altar and guest stars like Connor Paolo, Katie Cassidy, and more.</p>

        <div class="content">
            <h3>
                <a href="http://www.popsugar.com/Best-Gossip-Girl-Pictures-26291858" title="Say Farewell to Gossip Girl With a Look Back at the Cast&#039;s Cutest Snaps! " class="ga-track" data-ga-category="river" data-ga-action="clickthrough">
                    <span itemprop="headline">Say Farewell to Gossip Girl With a Look Back at the Cast's Cutest Snaps! </span>
                </a>
            </h3>
            <div class="excerpt">
                Tonight one of TV's most fashionable series comes to an end when Gossip Girl airs its final episode  check out pictures from the finale now.
            </div>
            <div class="post-content clearfix">

                <span class="byline standard" itemprop="author">
    <span itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <span class="author-image ws-attribute" data-ws-key="author_image" data-ws-target="style" style="background-image: url(http://media2.onsugar.com/files/2010/10/39/5/84/845155/avatar-medium-845155.jpg);" height="40" width="40"></span> <span class="ws-attribute" data-ws-key="author_byline" itemprop="name">by <a href="http://www.popsugar.com/author/Katie%20Henry" rel="author" itemprop="name">Katie Henry</a></span>
            </span>
</span>
                                    <div class="post-image">
                        <a href="http://www.popsugar.com/Best-Gossip-Girl-Pictures-26291858" title="Say Farewell to Gossip Girl With a Look Back at the Cast&#039;s Cutest Snaps! " class="ga-track" data-ga-category="river" data-ga-action="clickthrough">
                            <img itemprop="thumbnailUrl" alt="Say Farewell to Gossip Girl With a Look Back at the Cast&#039;s Cutest Snaps! " title="Say Farewell to Gossip Girl With a Look Back at the Cast&#039;s Cutest Snaps! " src="http://media3.onsugar.com/files/2012/12/50/5/192/1922398/blakeleighton.xxxlarge/i/Best-Gossip-Girl-Pictures.jpg">
                        </a>
                    </div>
                
                <div itemprop="articleBody">
                    <p>Tonight one of TV's most fashionable series comes to an end when <b>Gossip Girl</b> airs its final episode  check out <a href="http://www.buzzsugar.com/Gossip-Girl-Series-Finale-Pictures-26187387" >pictures from the finale</a> now. We'll have to wait and see if Chuck and Blair finally walk down the aisle, what happens between Serena and Dan, and the identity of Gossip Girl, but until then, we're taking a look back at some of the cast's best snaps over the past five years. </p>
<p>We've got on-set kisses, to industry parties and red-carpet affairs. Click through to see <a class="sugar_inline_link" title="Latest photos and news for Blake Lively" href="http://www.popsugar.com/Blake-Lively" target="_blank">Blake Lively</a>, <a class="sugar_inline_link" title="Latest photos and news for Leighton Meester" href="http://www.popsugar.com/Leighton-Meester" target="_blank">Leighton Meester</a>, <a class="sugar_inline_link" title="Latest photos and news for Penn Badgley" href="http://www.popsugar.com/Penn-Badgley" target="_blank">Penn Badgley</a>, and the rest of the Upper East Siders before we bid them a final farewell! </p>
<p>XOXO, PopSugar</p>

                </div>

    var user_experience;

    var trackingUrl = '';
    var enhancedTrackingUrl = trackingUrl;
    var _gaq = _gaq || [];

    window.trackerNames = [];

    
    (function () {
        window.overrideReferrer = false;
        if (window.ONSUGAR && ONSUGAR.Util) {
            var cookie = ONSUGAR.Util.getCookie('sugarSSOReferrer');
            if (cookie !== null) {
                window.overrideReferrer = cookie;
                ONSUGAR.Util.deleteCookie('sugarSSOReferrer');
            }
        }

        if (window.SUGAR && SUGAR.TestSettings) {
            if (typeof SUGAR.TestSettings.getRunSSOTest === 'function' && SUGAR.TestSettings.getRunSSOTest()) {
                ONSUGAR.Event.registerEventHandler('groupSelected', function() {
                    SUGAR.ABTest.trackPageView();
                });
            }
            else if (typeof SUGAR.TestSettings.getRunNoSSOTest() === 'function' && SUGAR.TestSettings.getRunNoSSOTest()) {
                SUGAR.ABTest.trackPageView();
            }
        }
